\documentclass[10pt]{article}
\usepackage[margin=0.6in,landscape]{geometry}
\usepackage{longtable, booktabs, array, pifont, multirow, seqsplit}
\newcommand{\cmark}{\ding{51}}
\newcommand{\xmark}{\ding{55}}
\newcommand{\fastkernels}{FastKernels}

\begin{document}

\section*{Manual review (preview, partial) --- HF Transformers $\to$ \fastkernels{} mapping}

\noindent
\textbf{Preview only:} this table is generated from audit batches 1--12 (out of 16 total).
Statuses come from the canonical CSV
(\texttt{\seqsplit{hf\_architecture\_operator\_coverage.csv}}); per-class kb-nano file
mappings come from the per-folder JSON dumps produced by the audit pipeline.
Format follows the previously-approved 10-row mentor review (Option C: one row
per HF compute class, multirow folder + status cells).

\textbf{Status legend:} $\bullet$ kb-nano L4 pipeline file exists in
\texttt{\seqsplit{tasks/baseline/L4/}}; \cmark{} every required kernel exists, only L4
wiring remains; \textbf{P} partial; \xmark{} unsupported; NIR
not-inference-required.

\textbf{Mapping legend:} a single \texttt{L<n>/file.py} = direct kernel match;
\texttt{\{file1, file2\}} = composes from listed files;
\textit{composes (wiring)} = pure structural class with no own kernel
(its forward is just composition of the kernels in classes it contains).
``inherits \texttt{ParentClass}'' is appended when the HF class subclasses a
class from a different architecture (cross-arch reuse signal).

{\scriptsize
\setlength{\tabcolsep}{4pt}
\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.18}
\begin{longtable}{@{}p{2.5cm} c p{6.0cm} p{12.0cm}@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{HF folder} & \textbf{Status} & \textbf{HF class} & \textbf{\fastkernels{} mapping} \\
\midrule
\endfirsthead
\multicolumn{4}{l}{\small\textit{(continued)}} \\
\toprule
\textbf{HF folder} & \textbf{Status} & \textbf{HF class} & \textbf{\fastkernels{} mapping} \\
\midrule
\endhead
\bottomrule
\endfoot

&& \texttt{AfmoeRMSNorm} & \texttt{L1/\allowbreak rms\_norm.py} \quad (inherits \texttt{GptOssRMSNorm}) \\
&& \texttt{AfmoeMLP} & \texttt{L2/\allowbreak llama\_mlp.py} \quad (inherits \texttt{Qwen2MoeMLP}) \\
&& \texttt{\seqsplit{AfmoeTokenChoiceRouter}} & \textit{composes (wiring)} \\

&& \texttt{\seqsplit{AfmoeSparseMoeBlock}} & \texttt{L2/\allowbreak shared\_expert\_moe.py} \\

&& \texttt{\seqsplit{RTDetrDecoderLayer}} & \textit{composes (wiring)} \\
